RNAMS LA SNGAR BZHIN DU RANG RANG GI RIGS KYI DBANG GIS RANG RANG
GI PHYOGS RNAMS SU'O, ,DUS KYI 'KHOR LO LA SOGS PA'I DE BZHIN
GSHEGS PA RNAMS LAS GZHAN PA'I LHA

RNAMS THAMS CAD RIN PO CHE SNA TSOGS KYI COD PAN CAN NO, ,'DIR
GANG GI TSE BCOM LDAN 'DAS DPAL DUS KYI 'KHOR LO RDO RJE SEMS
DPA'I NGO BOR RNAM PAR BZHAG NA DE'I TSE MI BSKYOD PA LJANG GU'I
MDOG GIS RGYAS BTAB PA'O, ,DE BZHIN DU SNA TSOGS YUM GANG GI TSE
MI BSKYOD PA'I RANG BZHIN DE'I TSE MI

BSKYOD PA SNGON PO GZUGS KYI RDO RJE SEMS DPAS SO, ,DE BZHIN DU
SNA TSOGS YUM RDO RJE DBYINGS KYI DBANG PHYUG MA'I RANG BZHIN NO,
,DE LTAR NA YE SHES DANG RNAM PAR SHES PA GNYIS LA PHAN TSUN
RGYAS BTAB PAR 'GYUR RO, ,DE SKAD DU DRI MA MED PA'I 'OD LAS,
RGYAL BA'I BDAG PO'I MCHOG NI YE SHES KYI PHUNG

PO'O; ,SNA TSOGS YUM GYI RNAM PAR SHES PA'I KHAMS SO, ,RNAM PAR
SHES PA NI NAM MKHA'I KHAMS SO ZHES GSUNGS SO, ,'DIR YE SHES NI
STONG PA NYID DANG SNYING RJE RO GCIG PA'I MI 'GYUR BA'I BDE BA
CHEN PO'I YE SHES SO, ,GANG GI TSE DUS KYI 'KHOR LO RNAM PAR SHES
PA'I PHUNG PO DE'I TSE SNA TSOGS YUM

NAM MKHA'I KHAMS RDO RJE DBYINGS KYI DBANG PHYUG MA'I RANG BZHIN
NO ZHES BYA BA'I DON TO, ,DE'I PHYIR GSUNGS PA 'KHYUD PAR 'GYUR
BA NI DO RJE DBYINGS KYI DBANG PHYUG MA SNA TSOGS YUM ZHES GSUNGS
SO, ,RDO RJE DBYINGS KYI DBANG PHYUG MA DANG LHAN CIG RNAM PAR
SHES PA PADMA'I SNYING PO LA BDE BA CHEN PO ZHES GSUNGS SO, ,DON
YOD GRUB

PA DANG; RIN CHEN 'BYUNG LDAN DANG, RNAM PAR SNANG MDZAD DANG,
'OD DPAG MED RNAMS NI MI BSKYOD PA LJANG GUS RGYAS BTAB PA'O,
,YANG NA DON YOD GRUB PA NI RIN CHEN 'BYUNG LDAN GYIS SO, ,RIN
CHEN 'BYUNG LDAN NI SNANG BA MTHA' YAS KYIS SO, ,DE NI RNAM PAR
SNANG MDZAD KYIS SO, ,DE NI MI BSKYOD PA LJANG GUS SO, ,KUN DU

@151A *, ,BZANG PO DANG, SGRA RDO RJE MA DANG, GNOD MDZES RGYAL
PO DANG, SHIN TU SNGON MO DANG, SNGON MO DANG, DRAG MO DANG,
RMUGS BYED DANG, RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I KLU RNAMS NI MI BSKYOD PA
SNGON PO'I GZUGS KYI RDO RJE SEMS DPAS RGYAS BTAB BA RNAMS SO,
,PHYAG NA RDO RJE DANG CHOS KYI DBYINGS KYI RDO RJE MA DANG,
GTZUG TOR

'KHOR LOS SGYUR BA DANG, DRAG MIG MA DANG, KHYAB 'JUG MA DANG,
GSHIN RJE DANG, RGYAL BA'I KLU NI MI BSKYOD PA LJANG GUS SO, ,LHA
GZHAN NAG PO RNAMS NI DON YOD GRUB PAS SO, ,DMAR PO RNAMS NI RIN
CHEN 'BYUNG LDAN GYIS SO, ,SER PO RNAMS NI RNAM PAR SNANG MDZAD
KYIS SO, ,DKAR PO RNAMS NI SNANG

BA MTHA' YAS KYIS SO, ,RGYAS 'DEBS PA'I DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA DRUG
PO 'DI DAG NI GTZUG TOR DANG BCAS PA, SNAM SBYAR 'DZIN PAS GNON
LA SOGS PA'I PHYAG RGYA DANG LDAN PA'O, ,BCOM LDAN 'DAS DKYIL
'KHOR GYI DBANG BO'I THUGS KA'I SA BON NI H'Um NGO, ,SNGAGS GZHAN
RNAMS NI MANGS BAS

'JIGS PAS MA BRIS SO, ,DE LTAR BSHAD PAR BYA MOD KYI, ,PHUN TSOGS
SKU NI DPAG MED DE, ,RGYA MTSO LA NI CHU 'DZIN GYIS, ,CHU BLANGS
ZAD PAR MI 'GYUR RO, ,RDO RJE 'DZIN DPAL SKU YI BDUD RTZI'I CHU
RGYUN LAS, ,'DOR BAR BYAS PA'I BSOD NAMS BDUD RTZI'I TSOGS KYIS
NI, ,DPAG MED SKU YI RLABS NI

RIM PAR BRGYUD PA YIS, ,MKHAS PA'I DBANG PHYUG 'JIGS MED GZHAN
DON BYED GYUR CIG, ,RDO RJE PHAG MOS MNGON SUM DU BYIN GYIS
BRLABS PA'I PAndI TA CHEN PO 'JIGS MED 'BYUNG GNAS SPAS PA'I ZHAL
SNGA NAS MDZAD PA RDZOGS PA'I RNAL 'BYOR GYI PHRENG BA ZHES BYA
BA RDZOGS SO,, ,,'DI'I GZHUNG TSAD

NI STONG NYIS BRGYA BZHUGS SO, ,RGYA GAR GYI PAndI TA CHEN PO
THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA'I DPAL BZANG POS 'GYUR RNYING PA LA BRTEN NAS
SMON 'GRO'I GTZUG LAG KHANG DU RANG 'GYUR MDZAD PA'O,, ,,PAndI TA
DE NYID KYIS LAN GNYIS SU ZHUS SHING GTUGS SO, ,SLAD KYI RGYA GAR
GYI PAndI TA CHEN

PO MKHAS BTZUN MCHOG GI GRUB PA BRNYES PA, BLA MA RJE BTZUN CHEN
PO RATNA RAKshI TA'I ZHABS DANG, BLA MA RJE BTZUN PAndI TA CHEN
PO RE BENDRA'I ZHAL SNGA NAS, CHAG LO TZ'A BA SH'AKYA'I DGE SLONG
DPAL GYI MTHA' CAN GYIS ZHUS SHING DAG PAR BSGYUR TE GTAN LA PHAB
PA'O,, ,,
